                        <div class="attribution">
                         <p class="Text-c11n-8-11-1__aiai24-0 kJZpve">
                          <strong>
                           About the ratings:
                          </strong>
                          GreatSchools ratings are designed to be a starting point to help parents compare schools, and should not be the only factor used in selecting the right school for your family. Zillow recommends that parents tour multiple schools in-person to inform that choice. Historically, GreatSchools ratings have been based solely on a comparison of standardized test results for all schools in a given state. As of September 2017, GreatSchools ratings also incorporate additional information, when available, such as college readiness, academic progress, advanced courses, equity, discipline and attendance data.
                          <a href="http://www.greatschools.org/gk/ratings/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                           Learn more
                          </a>
                         </p>

Check with the applicable school district prior to making a decision based on these boundaries. In addition, school data is obtained from a third party vendor and not guaranteed to be accurate, up to date or complete.

                    </span>
                    See a Zestimate jump? The Zestimate can change when the home is listed for sale, the home facts are updated, or the market fluctuates.
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div id="greatSchoolTooltip">
                  <div class="zsg-tooltip zsg-tooltip_animating zsg-tooltip_align-right" style="transform-origin: left 20px 0px;">
                   <div class="zsg-tooltip-content">
                    <a class="zsg-icon-x-thick zsg-tooltip-close-no-handler" role="button" tabindex="0">
                    </a>
                    <span class="zsg-tooltip-arrow">
                    </span>
                    <div>
                     GreatSchools ratings are designed to be a starting point to help parents compare schools, and should not be the only factor used in selecting the right school for your family. Zillow recommends that parents tour multiple schools in-person to inform that choice. Historically, GreatSchools ratings have been based solely on a comparison of standardized test results for all schools in a given state. As of September 2017, GreatSchools ratings also incorporate additional information, when available, such as college readiness, academic progress, advanced courses, equity, discipline and attendance data.
                     <a href="https://www.greatschools.org/gk/ratings/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                      Learn More.
                     </a>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                     The typical Zestimate
                     <sup>
                      
                     </sup>
                     valuation for a given geographic area on a given day is the

                      Zillow Home Value Index.

                     </a>
